For example, if you have 2 empty free cells and one empty column you can move at most 4 cards at a time.\r\n‚úì If you cannot move a stack because it is too large you can try splitting it into two parts. The game and its variants are popular in many countries and under various names.\r\n\r\nParchisi originated in India by the 6th century. \r\n\r\nEach player rolls the die; the highest roller begins the game. To enter a token into play from its yard to its starting square, a player must roll a 6. If the player has no tokens yet in play and rolls other than a 6, the turn passes to the next player.
